! Place names

! Continuation lexica
! ===================

! Some of the entries point to continuation lexica in the sme-lex.txt
! file, such as GOAHTI. This implies that names have the same inflection as
! ordinary nouns, which is probably not true. These lexica must thus be re-
! vised as soon as the lexica for names become more accurate.


! Continuation lexica for personal names
! --------------------------------------



! Vowel final names
! - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON ACCRA ! Vowel-final names without Gradation
! These sublexica are irrelevant for ACCRA, but added
! for the sake of the lexicon MARJA
 ACCRA-NE ;
 ACCRA-I ;
 ACCRA-OBL ;
 ACCRA-IICASE ;


LEXICON MARJA ! Vowel-final names with Gradation
 ACCRA-NE ;
 :X3 ACCRA-I ;
 :X4 ACCRA-OBL ;
 :X5 ACCRA-IICASE ;

LEXICON ACCRA-NE
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:n K ;

LEXICON ACCRA-I
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:j K ;

LEXICON ACCRA-OBL
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:# R ; ! for placenames
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:s K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:t K ;

LEXICON ACCRA-IICASE
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:jdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:jgujn K ;


! Vowel-final names where the final vowel carries
! primary or secondary stress. Monosyllables and
! Scandinavian stressed compounds in -V belong here.
LEXICON NYSTØ
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a# R ; ! for placenames
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:aj K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:an K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:ajde K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:ajgujn K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:'1a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:'1a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:'1aj K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:'1as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:'1ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:'an K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:'1at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:'1ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:'1ajd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:'1ajde K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:'1ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:'1ajgujn K ;



! Consonant-filal names
! - - - - - - - - - - -

LEXICON CNAME
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom:# R ; ! for place names
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a R ; ! for place names
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc+isuf:is K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com+isuf:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess+isuf:in K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc+asuf:as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com+asuf:ajn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess+asuf:an K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:ijdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:ijgujn K ;
!checking for i- and a-base suffixes.


! Finnish Itkonen, lexicon for Finnish nen-names
LEXICON C-FI-NEN
 :nen3 CNAME ; ! In Norway, they are declined as CNAME
               ! with ordinary genitive Itkonena
 :s FI-S ;     ! In Finland, they are declined with
               ! Itkosa as the oblique stem.

! Finnish Itkosa
LEXICON FI-S
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:# R ; ! For names
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:is K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:in K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:at K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:ijd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:ijdda K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:ijgujn K ;



LEXICON LONDON ! Final foot structure (X.) and (X..) => Loc:is

 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:is K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ijn K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:in K ;

LEXICON BERN ! Final foot structure (X) => Loc:as

 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Nom: R ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Gen:a R ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Acc:a K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Ill:ij K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Loc:as K ;
 +N+Prop+Sg+Com:ain K ;
 +N+Prop+Ess:an K ;

!LEXICON DUOMIS
! +N+Prop:X4 MALIS0 ;
! +N+Prop:X8 MALES ;
! +N+Prop:X2 MALLAS- ;

! the Heandarat lexicon is situatid in the sme-lex.txt file.


! Plural lexica
! -------------

LEXICON ALEUHTAT
 +N+Prop+Ess:n K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:X4t K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl:X5 ALEUHTAT-OBL ;

LEXICON ALEUHTAT-OBL
 +N+Prop+Pl+Gen:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Acc:jd K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Ill:jde K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Loc:jn K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Com:jgujn K ;

LEXICON SULLOT
 +N+Prop+Ess:X4n K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl+Nom:Y5t K ;
 +N+Prop+Pl:Y6 ALEUHTAT-OBL ;






! The lexica
! ==========

LEXICON ProperNoun
